## Page 2

<span style="font-family:'FZLTZHK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.50pt;color:#2f3582">内容简介</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">这是一本系统介绍和深度解读MCP的著作,旨</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">在为不同背景、不同需求的各类读者提供全面、实</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">用的指导。本书由MCP领域的
5位技术专家、布道</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">者撰写,他们各自发挥所长,从
10余个维度对MCP</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">进行了全面、透彻、深入的讲解。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">全书共11章,从技术、生态、商业
3大维度,深</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">入解析MCP如何重塑AI应用生态。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">第
1章回顾AI Agent的发展历程,揭示传统</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent的局限性及互联化挑战,提出MCP是突破瓶</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">颈的最优解。第
2章深度拆解MCP的技术内核,涵</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">盖设计目标、Function Call与RAG等关键概念,以</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">及MCP的架构实现原理。第
3章构建MCP生态的系</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">统全景图,分析参与者角色、合作模式及多场景应</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">用案例。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">第
4章和第
5章提供完整的开发指南:从MCP</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">主机端部署、代码运行器/邮件服务器等核心组件开</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">发,到客户端构建方法;结合Cherry Studio、腾</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">讯云等平台实战案例,演示AI Agent应用开发全流</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">程。第
6章聚焦行业变革,剖析MCP对Agently等主</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">流Agent框架的重构效应,以及对AI Agent平台架</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">构的颠覆性影响。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">第7~9章从宏观角度揭示MCP的产业价值:</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP驱动AI Agent从辅助工具向独立参与者进化;</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP改变大模型公司商业模式,促进技术普惠;规</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">划MCP客户端发展路径与商业化策略。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">第10~11章展望AI Agent互联网的未来,探讨</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP在智能社会中的核心地位,并前瞻性地分析</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP与A2A等协议的竞争融合趋势,揭示智能系统</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">演进的底层逻辑。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">本书兼具技术深度与产业视野,既是开发者构</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">建MCP应用的实操手册,也是从业者理解智能生态</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">变革的战略指南。通过揭示AI Agent互联网的技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">基座与商业图景,为读者提供参与下一代人工智能</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">浪潮的关键认知框架。</span>

## Page 5

<span style="font-family:'FelixTitlingMT';font-size:7.00pt;color:#42c8f4">P r e f a c e</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZXBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:20.00pt;color:#00aeef">前  言</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZY3K--GBK1-0';font-size:13.00pt;color:#00aeef">为何写作本书</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">自</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2022</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">12</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月以来,大模型和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">(智能体)以前所未有的速度从纯理论概念转</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">变为实际应用,并广泛渗透到各行各业的不同场景之中。我们见证了大模型和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 在</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">能力上的巨大飞跃,同时也目睹了其在实际应用中的蓬勃生机。然而,在这片繁荣景象的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">背后,一个隐形壁垒逐渐显现:不同的大模型、各式各样的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、海量的外部数据源</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">以及层出不穷的工具,有如散落的群岛,彼此孤立,难以实现高效的协同合作。这种隔绝</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">状态不仅大大增加了跨</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 和跨工具调用与数据发现的成本,也使得整个行业面临一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">个亟待突破的瓶颈。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">直到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2024</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">11</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Anthropic</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 公司提出并开源了模型上下文协议(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Model Context Protocol, </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">),这项技术标准的发布像是划破沉寂的号角,宣告了一个大模型、智能体、工具、数</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">据</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">API</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">SaaS</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 乃至桌面软件互联互通的新纪元的来临。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的诞生,恰似互联网破晓时分</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">HTTP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,它为构建一个支持</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 自由协作、无缝沟通的“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网”奠定了</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">基石,使人类驾驭</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 以应对复杂挑战的宏伟蓝图拥有了坚实的底层支撑。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的出现,如同一块投入平静湖面的巨石,激起了层层涟漪。无数热切目光汇聚于</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">此</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">无论是锐意创新的开发者、运筹帷幄的产品经理、洞察先机的企业决策者、寻求机</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">遇的投资人,还是记录时代的自媒体人,无不被</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所描绘的无限可能深深吸引。尤其是</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">对于通过编排、调度多个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 服务器以协同完成复杂任务,各个行业更是充满了实践的向</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">往,甚至视其为实现</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 场景化应用落地的最佳捷径。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">然而,当前关于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的系统性介绍与深度解读凤毛麟角,令许多满怀热情的探索者</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 望而却步,不知从何入手。鉴于此,本书应运而生。我们旨在为不同背景、不同需</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">求的读者</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">从开发者到决策者,从投资人到运营专员,从产品经理到内容创作者</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">提</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">供一本全面、深入且实用的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 指南。本书将引领读者,先从宏观视角洞察</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所引发</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的深远影响与其昭示的未来价值,再深入微观层面,剖析在真实场景中构建、部署与应用</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 服务器的具体案例和实操步骤,力求满足每一位读者借力</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 实现</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 应用落地的迫</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">切需求。</span>

## Page 6

<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IV</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZY3K--GBK1-0';font-size:13.00pt;color:#00aeef">本书主要内容</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">本书共</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">11</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章,内容涵盖</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网的演进、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的核心功能与技术实现、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的生态系统与发展趋势,以及如何构建基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的应用,并深入探讨</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 应用生</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">态、大模型公司、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 框架的影响,最后展望</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网的未来。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章回顾</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的发展历程,从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的发展与局限性,到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联如</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">何推动</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的普及,再到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网面临的挑战,以及</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 如何成为解决这些</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">挑战的最优解。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章深入解析</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的设计目标、相关概念(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Function Call</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">RAG</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">),以及</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">实现中的架构、组件与工作原理。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章探讨</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 生态系统的参与者、合作模式、发展策略、关键组成部分,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AI Agent</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章提供构建基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 应用的理论基础和实战指南,包括安装</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">主机端、</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章通过实际案例,展示在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Cherry Studio</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Clinde</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Cursor</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Cline</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 以及腾讯云等平</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">6</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章分析</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 对经典</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 框架(如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agently</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">BISHENG</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)核心组件的影响,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">7</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章探讨</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 应用生态的短期和长期影响,包括</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 从协助者到独立参</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">与者的转变、工具生态的无限扩展,以及通用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 在垂直领域中的应用潜力。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">8</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章分析</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 如何改变大模型公司的商业模式、促进大模型公司之间的合作与竞</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">争,以及推动大模型技术的普及与应用。</span>

## Page 14

<span style="font-family:'FelixTitlingMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#42c8f4">C H A P T E R   1</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#42c8f4">第</span><span style="font-family:'BodoniMT';font-size:24.00pt;color:#42c8f4">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZBYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#42c8f4"> 章</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:20.00pt;font-weight:bold;color:#00aeef">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZXBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:20.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 互联网的演进</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网的演进,是从孤立走向协作的技术变革。早期的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 功能单一,难以互</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">联;如今</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">DeepSeek-R1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">LangChain</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AutoGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 等正在推动</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 多元协作和自主决策时代的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">到来。但是,当前的“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网”仍面临标准缺失、安全和隐私风险等挑战。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的出现,如同破晓之光,为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 提供了跨平台的统一标准,搭建起</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 与现实世界的桥梁。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">过去</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“各自为政”,未来</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 将拆除“围墙”,实现无障碍协作。标准统一、安全可控、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">支持模块化扩展的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网,将引领下一次科技浪潮,让智能触手可及,让世界更</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">高效、更美好。</span>
<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:13.00pt;color:#00aeef">1.1</span><span style="font-family:'FZY3K--GBK1-0';font-size:13.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:13.00pt;color:#00aeef">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZY3K--GBK1-0';font-size:13.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 的发展与局限性</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">(人工智能)正在迅速发展,智能系统已广泛应用于各行各业。其中,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">作</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">为一种新兴技术范式,因具备更强的自主性和能动性,受到广泛关注。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 是能够自</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">主“感知</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">–</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 思考</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">–</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 执行”的智能程序,相比传统的被动式</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,更能适应复杂多变的环境。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">尤其在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> GPT-4 </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">等强大模型的推动下,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的能力和影响力正在不断提升。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">然而,如果我们只关注当下的技术进展,往往会忽视一个关键问题:</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">是如何</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">一步步发展到今天的?回顾它的演进历程,不仅有助于理解当前的技术水平,也能为判断</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">未来的发展方向提供重要参考。表</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1-1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 列示了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AI Agent </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的发展时间线与关键贡献者。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">时间</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">事件</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">/</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 贡献</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">关键贡献者</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1941</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1950</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">首创机器智能思想,提出图灵测试</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">阿兰·图灵(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Alan Turing</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1955</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1957</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">开发逻辑理论家和通用问题求解器(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">GPS</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">),提出物</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">理符号系统假说</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">艾伦· 纽厄尔(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Allen Newell</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">赫伯特·西蒙(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Herbert Simon</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1975</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">分布式人工智能(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">DAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)作为子领域出现</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">—</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1980</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">发表论文《合同网协议:分布式问题求解中的高级</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">通信与控制》,奠定</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">DAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 基础</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">里德·史密斯(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Reid Smith</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1989</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">MAAMAW</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 研讨会召开,推进多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 系统研究</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">约阿夫·肖汉(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Yoav Shoham</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">出版《人工智能:一种现代的方法》,正式定义</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">AI </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">斯图尔特·罗素(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Stuart Russell</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">彼得·诺维格(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Peter Norvig</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">2023</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">全球发布多个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">LLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">(如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Llama</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">BLOOM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">StableLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">ChatGLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 等)</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Meta</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">BigScience</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Stability AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">智谱清言等</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">2023</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">OpenAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 发布</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">GPT-4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">AutoGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 问世,展示</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">新潜力</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">OpenAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、托兰·布鲁斯·理查德</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">兹(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Toran Bruce Richards</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">)</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">2023</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月后</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">涌现</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Generative Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">GPT-Engineer</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">BabyAGI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">MetaGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 等项目</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">全球开发者社区</span>
<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">1.1.1</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 的起源与演化</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 是指一种能够感知环境、自主决策并采取行动以实现特定目标的智能系统。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">作为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 领域的核心概念之一,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的发展经历了多个阶段,汇聚了众多研究者的重要</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">贡献。其定义和内涵随着技术演进不断深化,涵盖了从早期的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AI </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">理论探索到现代多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">系统的广泛研究。</span>
<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">1. 20</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">50</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">—</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">60</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 年代:</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 的起源</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的概念可以追溯到人工智能的早期阶段,特别是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">50</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">60</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年代的开创</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">性工作。在这一时期,艾伦·纽厄尔(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Allen Newell</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)和赫伯特·西蒙(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Herbert Simon</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)是</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">关键人物。他们开发了逻辑理论家(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Logic Theorist</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1955</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年)和通用问题求解器(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">General </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Problem Solver</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1957</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年)等程序,这些程序能够解决复杂问题并进行决策,可以看作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的雏形。他们的物理符号系统假说(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Physical Symbol System Hypothesis</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)提出,任</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">何能够操作符号的系统都具备实现智能行为所需的充分必要条件。这一假说在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1976</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">图灵奖讲座中得到明确阐述,定义了“机器”作为操作符号的代理,这一定义为后来的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 概念奠定了理论基础。尽管他们可能并未直接使用“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">”这一术语,但他们的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">工作为这一概念的形成提供了重要的理论支持。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">阿兰·图灵(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Alan Turing</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1941</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年开始思考机器智能。他在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1950</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年发表的论文《计</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">算机器与智能》中提出了著名的“图灵测试”作为评估机器智能的标准。该测试让人类评</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">判者与机器进行文字对话,并要求人类评判者判断对话对象是人类还是机器。如果机器的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">回答无法被区分为非人类的,那么就认为机器具备了智能。图灵强调,应通过行为表现而</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">非内部机制来判断机器是否具备智能,这一观点对后来的人工智能研究产生了深远影响。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">尽管图灵未明确使用“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">”一词,但他的工作为智能系统的自主行为提供了哲学和理论</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">基础。</span>
<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">2. 20</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">70</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">—</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">80</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 年代:分布式人工智能兴起</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">70</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">80</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年代,分布式人工智能(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Distributed Artificial Intelligence</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">DAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)作为</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20">(续)</span>

---

## Page 16

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的一个子领域兴起,标志着</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 概念的进一步发展。根据记录,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">DAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1975</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年被</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">正式提出,主要关注</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 之间的交互,分为多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 系统和分布式问题解决两大分支。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">这一时期的研究重点是多个智能实体如何通过合作、共存或竞争来解决问题。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1980</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年,里德·史密斯(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Reid Smith</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)发表了论文《合同网协议:分布式问题求解中的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">高级通信与控制》(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">The Contract Net Protocol</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> :</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">High-Level Communication and Control in A </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Distributed Problem Solver</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">),这篇论文被认为是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">DAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的重要里程碑。它提出了一个分布式</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">任务分配框架,框架中的多个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 通过通信协调完成任务。这一工作为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的分</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">布式特性提供了实践基础,尽管当时可能未明确使用“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">”这一术语。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">这一时期的另一贡献是卡尔·休伊特(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Carl Hewitt</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">70</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年代提出的演员模型</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Actor Model</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">),该模型描述了并发计算中的自主实体通过消息传递进行交互。虽然演员模</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">型主要用于并发系统,但其思想与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的自主性和交互性有着密切的联系。</span>
<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">3. 20</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">90</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 年代:</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 范式的形成</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">到了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">90</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年代,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的概念被广泛接受,成为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 研究的核心框架。这一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">转变得益于决策理论、经济学的引入,以及多学科的交叉融合。根据“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> History of Artificial </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:3.50pt;color:#231f20">一</span><span style="font-family:'KoreanMJ-M';font-size:8.50pt;color:#231f20">○</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,这一时期的研究者如朱迪亚·珀尔(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Judea Pearl</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)、莱斯利·</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">P.</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 凯尔布林</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Intelligence</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">”</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Leslie P. Kaelbling</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)等人,将决策理论和经济学中的理性</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 概念引入</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,丰富了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的定义。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1993</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年,约阿夫·肖汉(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Yoav Shoham</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)发表了论文《面向</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的编程》(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent-</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Oriented Programming</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">),明确提出了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的正式定义,包括其信念、欲望和意图(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">BDI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 模</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">型),为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 理论框架的构建做出了重要贡献。这一时期还出现了针对多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 系统的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">研究,如欧洲多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 系统建模自主</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 研讨会从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1989</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年开始举办,进一步推动了相关</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">研究。</span>
<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">4. 1995</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">—</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">2022</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 年:现代定义与推广</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1995</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年,斯图尔特·罗素和彼得·诺维格出版了《人工智能:一种现代的方法》</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:10.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#231f20">Artificial Intelligence: A Modern Approach</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)一书。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">这本教科书成为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 领域的标准参考文献。他们将人工智能定义为“研究和设计</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的学科”,并明确了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的定义:任何能通过传感器感知环境并通过执行器采取</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">行动的实体。这一定义包括机器人、软件程序等,强调了目标导向行为是智能的核心。这</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">一工作标志着</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 概念的正式化和普及,为后来的研究奠定了基础。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">尽管罗素和诺维格的定义被广泛接受,但</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的概念在不同领域(如机器人、软</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">件</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 系统)中有不同的解释,存在一定争议,例如是否所有自主系统都应被</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">视为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,以及</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的智能程度如何定义。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:4.15pt;color:#231f20">一</span><span style="font-family:'KoreanMJ-M';font-size:10.50pt;color:#231f20">○</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">ALBERTO G, PATRICK J D, PHILIPPE C, et al. History of Artificial Intelligence [M] // FILIPPO F, OLIMPIO G, </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章 </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网的演进</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">  3</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>

## Page 17

<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">4  </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">一本书讲透</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MCP</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">:</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 互联网新纪元</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">着</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AI Agent </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">应用进入新阶段。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">自</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2023</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月起,全球多家科技公司陆续发布了自己的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">LLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,包括</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Llama</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">BLOOM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">StableLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">ChatGLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 等开源模型。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2023</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">14</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 日,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OpenAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 发布了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GPT-4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">,这一事件成</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">为当年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 发展的里程碑。紧随其后,当年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月底,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AutoGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 横空出世,迅速引发全球关注。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AutoGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 是由</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OpenAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GitHub</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 上推出的免费开源项目,结合了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GPT-4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GPT-3.5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 技术,</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">能通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">API</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 实现完整项目的创建。与传统的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">ChatGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 不同,用户无须持续提问,只需要提</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">供一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 名称、描述和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 个目标,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AutoGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 便可自主完成任务。它能够读写文件、浏览网</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">页、审查自身生成的结果,并结合历史记录进行优化。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AutoGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 展示了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GPT-4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的强大能力,</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">也为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的自主性树立了新标杆。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">作为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OpenAI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的实验性项目,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AutoGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 不仅吸引了技术社区的目光,也让更多人认识</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的潜力。这一事件成为催化剂,随后基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">LLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 项目如雨后春笋般</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">涌现,例如通用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GPT-Engineer</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">BabyAGI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MetaGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 等,这些创新使</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">LLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的发展</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">与应用进入全新阶段。这些项目的涌现不仅加速了技术进步,也将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">LLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的创业热潮和落地</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">实践引向了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的方向,预示着</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 在未来智能化社会中的核心地位。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的概念起源于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">50</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年代的理论探索,在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1995</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年由罗素和诺维格创作的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">经典教科书中被正式定义。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2023</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">LLM</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AutoGPT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的出现将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 推进到快速演化</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的新阶段。经过数十年发展,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 逐渐形成了下面的概念框架。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 是一种具备环境感知、自主决策和任务执行能力的智能系统。它能理解自然</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">语言指令,自主在互联网或软件环境中完成复杂任务。用户只需给出目标,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 即可</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">自动分解任务、调用工具、检索信息,最终完成任务。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的核心特征之一是自主性,</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">这使其能在无人工干预的情况下独立感知环境、做出决策并执行任务。与之并行的另一项</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">关键能力是基于大模型的推理,</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 依靠这一能力处理复杂数据,进行深度分析,以</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">制订最优行动方案。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">我们以智能电子邮件分类系统为例,介绍</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 最小框架,即包括感知(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Perception</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">模块、规划(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Planning</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)模块与行动(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Action</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">)模块的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">PPA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 模型,如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1-1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZXDXK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">(</span><span style="font-family:'Swiss721BT-Light';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZXDXK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">)感知</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 访问用户的电子邮件账户,</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">收集新邮件的发件人、主题、正文、附</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">件等信息,为后续决策提供数据基础。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZXDXK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">(</span><span style="font-family:'Swiss721BT-Light';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZXDXK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">)规划</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 首先依据预定分类标准</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">(如工作、个人、促销、社交)分析邮件特征,以确定邮件的类别,然后使用机器学习算法</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">(如朴素贝叶斯或支持向量机)进行模型训练,并设置分类阈值。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">感知模块</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">规划模块</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">策略</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">行动模块</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">AI Agent</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 最小框架:</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">PPA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 模型</span>
